				limit = { 
					OR = {

				holder_scope = {

					}
				}
			}
			c_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { year = 8197 } }
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.1.1={ 
		effect = {
			d_oldtown = {
				holder_scope = {
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			d_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	culture="reachman"

	mother=4010298

	add_trait=ambitious

	8129.4.1={ #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			set_character_flag = supporting_king
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}				
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
			}
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
						years = 5
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_with_king
						years = 100
					}
					ROOT = {
						join_defender_wars = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8129.4.1={ #Dance of the Dragons

			}

				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
						years = 5
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_with_king

				}
			}

				holder_scope = {

		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			set_character_flag = against_king
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}				
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
			}
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			c_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { year = 8197 } }
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.1.1={ 
		effect = {
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			d_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader

					}
				}
			}
		}

		add_trait="scholar"
		add_trait="erudite"
		effect = {
			c_summerhall = { holder_scope = { ROOT = { move_character = PREV } } }
		}
	}
	8259.1.1 = { #summerhall burnt, becomes archmaester
		remove_trait="maester"
		add_trait="archmaester"
		effect = {
			c_the_citadel = { holder_scope = { ROOT = { move_character = PREV } } }
		}
	}
	8285.1.1={ 
		death = yes
	}
}
